754}
755
756#endif // GET_REGISTER_MATCHER

759#ifdef GET_SUBTARGET_FEATURE_NAME
760#undef GET_SUBTARGET_FEATURE_NAME
761
762// User-level names for subtarget features that participate in
763// instruction matching.
764static const char *getSubtargetFeatureName(uint64_t Val) {
765 switch(Val) {
766 case Feature_HasStdExtMBit: return "'M' (Integer Multiplication and Division)";
767 case Feature_HasStdExtABit: return "'A' (Atomic Instructions)";
768 case Feature_HasStdExtFBit: return "'F' (Single-Precision Floating-Point)";
769 case Feature_HasStdExtDBit: return "'D' (Double-Precision Floating-Point)";
770 case Feature_HasStdExtZfhBit: return "'Zfh' (Half-Precision Floating-Point)";
771 case Feature_HasStdExtCBit: return "'C' (Compressed Instructions)";
772 case Feature_HasStdExtZbaBit: return "'Zba' (Address calculation 'B' Instructions)";
773 case Feature_HasStdExtZbbBit: return "'Zbb' (Base 'B' Instructions)";
774 case Feature_HasStdExtZbcBit: return "'Zbc' (Carry-Less 'B' Instructions)";
775 case Feature_HasStdExtZbeBit: return "'Zbe' (Extract-Deposit 'B' Instructions)";
776 case Feature_HasStdExtZbfBit: return "'Zbf' (Bit-Field 'B' Instructions)";
777 case Feature_HasStdExtZbmBit: return "'Zbm' (Matrix 'B' Instructions)";
778 case Feature_HasStdExtZbpBit: return "'Zbp' (Permutation 'B' Instructions)";
779 case Feature_HasStdExtZbrBit: return "'Zbr' (Polynomial Reduction 'B' Instructions)";
780 case Feature_HasStdExtZbsBit: return "'Zbs' (Single-Bit 'B' Instructions)";
781 case Feature_HasStdExtZbtBit: return "'Zbt' (Ternary 'B' Instructions)";
782 case Feature_HasStdExtZbbOrZbpBit: return "'Zbb' (Base 'B' Instructions) or 'Zbp' (Permutation 'B' Instructions)";
783 case Feature_HasStdExtZbproposedcBit: return "'Zbproposedc' (Proposed Compressed 'B' Instructions)";
784 case Feature_HasStdExtBBit: return "'B' (Bit Manipulation Instructions)";
785 case Feature_HasRVCHintsBit: return "RVC Hint Instructions";
786 case Feature_HasStdExtVBit: return "'V' (Vector Instructions)";
787 case Feature_HasStdExtZvlssegBit: return "'Zvlsseg' (Vector segment load/store instructions)";
788 case Feature_HasStdExtZvamoBit: return "'Zvamo'(Vector AMO Operations)";
789 case Feature_IsRV64Bit: return "RV64I Base Instruction Set";
790 case Feature_IsRV32Bit: return "RV32I Base Instruction Set";
791 case Feature_IsRV32EBit: return "";
792 default: return "(unknown)";
793 }
794}
795
796#endif // GET_SUBTARGET_FEATURE_NAME

802static void applyMnemonicAliases(StringRef &Mnemonic, const FeatureBitset &Features, unsigned VariantID) {
803 switch (VariantID) {
804 case 0:
805 switch (Mnemonic.size()) {
806 default: break;
807 case 4: // 1 string to match.
808 if (memcmp(Mnemonic.data()+0, "move", 4) != 0)
809 break;
810 Mnemonic = "mv"; // "move"
811 return;
812 case 5: // 1 string to match.
813 if (memcmp(Mnemonic.data()+0, "scall", 5) != 0)
814 break;
815 Mnemonic = "ecall"; // "scall"
816 return;
817 case 6: // 1 string to match.
818 if (memcmp(Mnemonic.data()+0, "sbreak", 6) != 0)
819 break;
820 Mnemonic = "ebreak"; // "sbreak"
821 return;
822 case 7: // 2 strings to match.
823 if (memcmp(Mnemonic.data()+0, "fmv.", 4) != 0)
824 break;
825 switch (Mnemonic[4]) {
826 default: break;
827 case 's': // 1 string to match.
828 if (memcmp(Mnemonic.data()+5, ".x", 2) != 0)
829 break;
830 if (Features.test(Feature_HasStdExtFBit)) // "fmv.s.x"
831 Mnemonic = "fmv.w.x";
832 return;
833 case 'x': // 1 string to match.
834 if (memcmp(Mnemonic.data()+5, ".s", 2) != 0)
835 break;
836 if (Features.test(Feature_HasStdExtFBit)) // "fmv.x.s"
837 Mnemonic = "fmv.x.w";
838 return;
839 }
840 break;
841 }
842 break;
843 }
844 switch (Mnemonic.size()) {
845 default: break;
846 case 4: // 1 string to match.
847 if (memcmp(Mnemonic.data()+0, "move", 4) != 0)
848 break;
849 Mnemonic = "mv"; // "move"
850 return;
851 case 5: // 1 string to match.
852 if (memcmp(Mnemonic.data()+0, "scall", 5) != 0)
853 break;
854 Mnemonic = "ecall"; // "scall"
855 return;
856 case 6: // 1 string to match.
857 if (memcmp(Mnemonic.data()+0, "sbreak", 6) != 0)
858 break;
859 Mnemonic = "ebreak"; // "sbreak"
860 return;
861 case 7: // 2 strings to match.
862 if (memcmp(Mnemonic.data()+0, "fmv.", 4) != 0)
863 break;
864 switch (Mnemonic[4]) {
865 default: break;
866 case 's': // 1 string to match.
867 if (memcmp(Mnemonic.data()+5, ".x", 2) != 0)
868 break;
869 if (Features.test(Feature_HasStdExtFBit)) // "fmv.s.x"
870 Mnemonic = "fmv.w.x";
871 return;
872 case 'x': // 1 string to match.
873 if (memcmp(Mnemonic.data()+5, ".s", 2) != 0)
874 break;
875 if (Features.test(Feature_HasStdExtFBit)) // "fmv.x.s"
876 Mnemonic = "fmv.x.w";
877 return;
878 }
879 break;
880 }
881}

1375
1376void RISCVAsmParser::
1377convertToMCInst(unsigned Kind, MCInst &Inst, unsigned Opcode,
1378 const OperandVector &Operands,
1379 const SmallBitVector &OptionalOperandsMask) {
1380 assert(Kind < CVT_NUM_SIGNATURES && "Invalid signature!");
1381 const uint8_t *Converter = ConversionTable[Kind];
1382 unsigned DefaultsOffset[8] = { 0 };
1383 assert(OptionalOperandsMask.size() == 7);
1384 for (unsigned i = 0, NumDefaults = 0; i < 7; ++i) {
1385 DefaultsOffset[i + 1] = NumDefaults;
1386 NumDefaults += (OptionalOperandsMask[i] ? 1 : 0);
1387 }
1388 unsigned OpIdx;
1389 Inst.setOpcode(Opcode);
1390 for (const uint8_t *p = Converter; *p; p += 2) {
1391 OpIdx = *(p + 1) - DefaultsOffset[*(p + 1)];
1392 switch (*p) {
1393 default: llvm_unreachable("invalid conversion entry!");
1394 case CVT_Reg:
1395 static_cast<RISCVOperand &>(*Operands[OpIdx]).addRegOperands(Inst, 1);
1396 break;
1397 case CVT_Tied: {
1398 assert(OpIdx < (size_t)(std::end(TiedAsmOperandTable) -
1399 std::begin(TiedAsmOperandTable)) &&
1400 "Tied operand not found");
1401 unsigned TiedResOpnd = TiedAsmOperandTable[OpIdx][0];
1402 if (TiedResOpnd != (uint8_t)-1)
1403 Inst.addOperand(Inst.getOperand(TiedResOpnd));
1404 break;
1405 }
1406 case CVT_95_Reg:
1407 static_cast<RISCVOperand &>(*Operands[OpIdx]).addRegOperands(Inst, 1);
1408 break;
1409 case CVT_95_addImmOperands:
1410 static_cast<RISCVOperand &>(*Operands[OpIdx]).addImmOperands(Inst, 1);
1411 break;
1412 case CVT_95_addRegOperands:
1413 static_cast<RISCVOperand &>(*Operands[OpIdx]).addRegOperands(Inst, 1);
1414 break;
1415 case CVT_regX0:
1416 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createReg(RISCV::X0));
1417 break;
1418 case CVT_imm_95_0:
1419 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(0));
1420 break;
1421 case CVT_95_addCSRSystemRegisterOperands:
1422 static_cast<RISCVOperand &>(*Operands[OpIdx]).addCSRSystemRegisterOperands(Inst, 1);
1423 break;
1424 case CVT_imm_95_7:
1425 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(7));
1426 break;
1427 case CVT_95_addFRMArgOperands:
1428 static_cast<RISCVOperand &>(*Operands[OpIdx]).addFRMArgOperands(Inst, 1);
1429 break;
1430 case CVT_imm_95_15:
1431 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(15));
1432 break;
1433 case CVT_95_addFenceArgOperands:
1434 static_cast<RISCVOperand &>(*Operands[OpIdx]).addFenceArgOperands(Inst, 1);
1435 break;
1436 case CVT_imm_95_3:
1437 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(3));
1438 break;
1439 case CVT_imm_95_1:
1440 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(1));
1441 break;
1442 case CVT_imm_95_2:
1443 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(2));
1444 break;
1445 case CVT_regX1:
1446 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createReg(RISCV::X1));
1447 break;
1448 case CVT_imm_95__MINUS_1:
1449 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(-1));
1450 break;
1451 case CVT_imm_95_31:
1452 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(31));
1453 break;
1454 case CVT_imm_95_63:
1455 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(63));
1456 break;
1457 case CVT_imm_95_16:
1458 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(16));
1459 break;
1460 case CVT_imm_95_48:
1461 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(48));
1462 break;
1463 case CVT_imm_95_30:
1464 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(30));
1465 break;
1466 case CVT_imm_95_62:
1467 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(62));
1468 break;
1469 case CVT_imm_95_6:
1470 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(6));
1471 break;
1472 case CVT_imm_95_14:
1473 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(14));
1474 break;
1475 case CVT_imm_95_32:
1476 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(32));
1477 break;
1478 case CVT_imm_95_28:
1479 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(28));
1480 break;
1481 case CVT_imm_95_60:
1482 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(60));
1483 break;
1484 case CVT_imm_95_4:
1485 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(4));
1486 break;
1487 case CVT_imm_95_12:
1488 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(12));
1489 break;
1490 case CVT_imm_95_24:
1491 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(24));
1492 break;
1493 case CVT_imm_95_56:
1494 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(56));
1495 break;
1496 case CVT_imm_95_8:
1497 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(8));
1498 break;
1499 case CVT_imm_95_3072:
1500 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(3072));
1501 break;
1502 case CVT_imm_95_3200:
1503 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(3200));
1504 break;
1505 case CVT_imm_95_3074:
1506 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(3074));
1507 break;
1508 case CVT_imm_95_3202:
1509 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(3202));
1510 break;
1511 case CVT_imm_95_3073:
1512 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(3073));
1513 break;
1514 case CVT_imm_95_3201:
1515 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(3201));
1516 break;
1517 case CVT_95_addRegOperands_95_defaultMaskRegOp:
1518 if (OptionalOperandsMask[*(p + 1) - 1]) {
1519 defaultMaskRegOp()->addRegOperands(Inst, 1);
1520 } else {
1521 static_cast<RISCVOperand &>(*Operands[OpIdx]).addRegOperands(Inst, 1);
1522 }
1523 break;
1524 case CVT_95_addVTypeIOperands:
1525 static_cast<RISCVOperand &>(*Operands[OpIdx]).addVTypeIOperands(Inst, 1);
1526 break;
1527 case CVT_imm_95_255:
1528 Inst.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(255));
1529 break;
1530 }
1531 }
1532}
1533
1534void RISCVAsmParser::
1535convertToMapAndConstraints(unsigned Kind,
1536 const OperandVector &Operands) {
1537 assert(Kind < CVT_NUM_SIGNATURES && "Invalid signature!");
1538 unsigned NumMCOperands = 0;
1539 const uint8_t *Converter = ConversionTable[Kind];
1540 for (const uint8_t *p = Converter; *p; p += 2) {
1541 switch (*p) {
1542 default: llvm_unreachable("invalid conversion entry!");
1543 case CVT_Reg:
1544 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1545 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("r");
1546 ++NumMCOperands;
1547 break;
1548 case CVT_Tied:
1549 ++NumMCOperands;
1550 break;
1551 case CVT_95_Reg:
1552 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1553 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("r");
1554 NumMCOperands += 1;
1555 break;
1556 case CVT_95_addImmOperands:
1557 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1558 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("m");
1559 NumMCOperands += 1;
1560 break;
1561 case CVT_95_addRegOperands:
1562 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1563 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("m");
1564 NumMCOperands += 1;
1565 break;
1566 case CVT_regX0:
1567 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1568 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("m");
1569 ++NumMCOperands;
1570 break;
1571 case CVT_imm_95_0:
1572 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1573 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("");
1574 ++NumMCOperands;
1575 break;
1576 case CVT_95_addCSRSystemRegisterOperands:
1577 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1578 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("m");
1579 NumMCOperands += 1;
1580 break;
1581 case CVT_imm_95_7:
1582 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1583 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("");
1584 ++NumMCOperands;
1585 break;
1586 case CVT_95_addFRMArgOperands:
1587 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1588 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("m");
1589 NumMCOperands += 1;
1590 break;
1591 case CVT_imm_95_15:
1592 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1593 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("");
1594 ++NumMCOperands;
1595 break;
1596 case CVT_95_addFenceArgOperands:
1597 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1598 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("m");
1599 NumMCOperands += 1;
1600 break;
1601 case CVT_imm_95_3:
1602 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1603 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("");
1604 ++NumMCOperands;
1605 break;
1606 case CVT_imm_95_1:
1607 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1608 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("");
1609 ++NumMCOperands;
1610 break;
1611 case CVT_imm_95_2:
1612 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1613 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("");
1614 ++NumMCOperands;
1615 break;
1616 case CVT_regX1:
1617 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1618 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("m");
1619 ++NumMCOperands;
1620 break;
1621 case CVT_imm_95__MINUS_1:
1622 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1623 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("");
1624 ++NumMCOperands;
1625 break;
1626 case CVT_imm_95_31:
1627 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1628 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("");
1629 ++NumMCOperands;
1630 break;
1631 case CVT_imm_95_63:
1632 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1633 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("");
1634 ++NumMCOperands;
1635 break;
1636 case CVT_imm_95_16:
1637 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1638 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("");
1639 ++NumMCOperands;
1640 break;
1641 case CVT_imm_95_48:
1642 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1643 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("");
1644 ++NumMCOperands;
1645 break;
1646 case CVT_imm_95_30:
1647 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1648 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("");
1649 ++NumMCOperands;
1650 break;
1651 case CVT_imm_95_62:
1652 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1653 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("");
1654 ++NumMCOperands;
1655 break;
1656 case CVT_imm_95_6:

1659 ++NumMCOperands;

1664 ++NumMCOperands;
1665 break;
1666 case CVT_imm_95_32:
1667 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1668 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("");
1669 ++NumMCOperands;
1670 break;
1671 case CVT_imm_95_28:

1673 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("");
1674 ++NumMCOperands;
1675 break;
1676 case CVT_imm_95_60:
1677 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1678 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("");
1679 ++NumMCOperands;
1680 break;

1683 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("");

1685 break;
1686 case CVT_imm_95_12:
1687 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1688 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("");

1695 break;

1699 ++NumMCOperands;
1700 break;

1705 break;

1708 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("");
1709 ++NumMCOperands;
1710 break;
1711 case CVT_imm_95_3200:
1712 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1713 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("");
1714 ++NumMCOperands;
1715 break;
1716 case CVT_imm_95_3074:
1717 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1718 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("");
1719 ++NumMCOperands;
1720 break;
1721 case CVT_imm_95_3202:
1722 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1723 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("");
1724 ++NumMCOperands;
1725 break;
1726 case CVT_imm_95_3073:
1727 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);

1729 ++NumMCOperands;
1730 break;

1734 ++NumMCOperands;
1735 break;
1736 case CVT_95_addRegOperands_95_defaultMaskRegOp:
1737 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1738 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("m");
1739 NumMCOperands += 1;
1740 break;
1741 case CVT_95_addVTypeIOperands:
1742 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setMCOperandNum(NumMCOperands);
1743 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("m");
1744 NumMCOperands += 1;
1745 break;

1748 Operands[*(p + 1)]->setConstraint("");
1749 ++NumMCOperands;
1750 break;
1751 }

1863
1864static unsigned getDiagKindFromRegisterClass(MatchClassKind RegisterClass) {
1865 return MCTargetAsmParser::Match_InvalidOperand;
1866}
1867
1868static MatchClassKind matchTokenString(StringRef Name) {
1869 switch (Name.size()) {
1870 default: break;
1871 case 1: // 2 strings to match.
1872 switch (Name[0]) {
1873 default: break;
1874 case '(': // 1 string to match.
1875 return MCK__40_; // "("
1876 case ')': // 1 string to match.
1877 return MCK__41_; // ")"
1878 }
1879 break;
1880 }
1881 return InvalidMatchClass;
1882}
1883
1884/// isSubclass - Compute whether \p A is a subclass of \p B.
1885static bool isSubclass(MatchClassKind A, MatchClassKind B) {
1886 if (A == B)
1887 return true;
1888
1889 switch (A) {
1890 default:
1891 return false;
1892
1893 case MCK_Reg55:
1894 return B == MCK_VRN8M1;
1895
1896 case MCK_Reg52:
1897 return B == MCK_VRN7M1;
1898
1899 case MCK_Reg49:
1900 return B == MCK_VRN6M1;
1901
1902 case MCK_Reg46:
1903 return B == MCK_VRN5M1;
1904
1905 case MCK_Reg43:
1906 return B == MCK_VRN4M2;
1907
1908 case MCK_Reg40:
1909 return B == MCK_VRN4M1;
1910
1911 case MCK_Reg37:
1912 return B == MCK_VRN3M2;
1913
1914 case MCK_Reg34:
1915 return B == MCK_VRN3M1;
1916
1917 case MCK_Reg31:
1918 return B == MCK_VRN2M4;
1919
1920 case MCK_Reg28:
1921 return B == MCK_VRN2M2;
1922
1923 case MCK_Reg25:
1924 return B == MCK_VRN2M1;
1925
1926 case MCK_Reg22:
1927 return B == MCK_VRM8;
1928
1929 case MCK_Reg19:
1930 return B == MCK_VRM4;
1931
1932 case MCK_Reg16:
1933 return B == MCK_VRM2;
1934
1935 case MCK_GPRX0:
1936 return B == MCK_GPR;
1937
1938 case MCK_SP:
1939 switch (B) {
1940 default: return false;
1941 case MCK_GPRNoX0: return true;
1942 case MCK_GPR: return true;
1943 }
1944
1945 case MCK_VMV0:
1946 return B == MCK_VR;
1947
1948 case MCK_VRM8NoV0:
1949 return B == MCK_VRM8;
1950
1951 case MCK_Reg33:
1952 return B == MCK_VRN2M4;
1953
1954 case MCK_Reg7:
1955 switch (B) {
1956 default: return false;
1957 case MCK_GPRC: return true;
1958 case MCK_GPRTC: return true;
1959 case MCK_GPRNoX0X2: return true;
1960 case MCK_GPRNoX0: return true;
1961 case MCK_GPR: return true;
1962 }
1963
1964 case MCK_VRM4NoV0:
1965 return B == MCK_VRM4;
1966
1967 case MCK_FPR32C:
1968 return B == MCK_FPR32;
1969
1970 case MCK_FPR64C:
1971 return B == MCK_FPR64;
1972
1973 case MCK_GPRC:
1974 switch (B) {
1975 default: return false;
1976 case MCK_GPRNoX0X2: return true;
1977 case MCK_GPRNoX0: return true;
1978 case MCK_GPR: return true;
1979 }
1980
1981 case MCK_Reg45:
1982 return B == MCK_VRN4M2;
1983
1984 case MCK_Reg39:
1985 return B == MCK_VRN3M2;
1986
1987 case MCK_Reg30:
1988 return B == MCK_VRN2M2;
1989
1990 case MCK_GPRTC:
1991 switch (B) {
1992 default: return false;
1993 case MCK_GPRNoX0X2: return true;
1994 case MCK_GPRNoX0: return true;
1995 case MCK_GPR: return true;
1996 }
1997
1998 case MCK_VRM2NoV0:
1999 return B == MCK_VRM2;
2000
2001 case MCK_Reg57:
2002 return B == MCK_VRN8M1;
2003
2004 case MCK_Reg54:
2005 return B == MCK_VRN7M1;
2006
2007 case MCK_Reg51:
2008 return B == MCK_VRN6M1;
2009
2010 case MCK_Reg48:
2011 return B == MCK_VRN5M1;
2012
2013 case MCK_Reg42:
2014 return B == MCK_VRN4M1;
2015
2016 case MCK_Reg36:
2017 return B == MCK_VRN3M1;
2018
2019 case MCK_Reg27:
2020 return B == MCK_VRN2M1;
2021
2022 case MCK_GPRNoX0X2:
2023 switch (B) {
2024 default: return false;
2025 case MCK_GPRNoX0: return true;
2026 case MCK_GPR: return true;
2027 }
2028
2029 case MCK_GPRNoX0:
2030 return B == MCK_GPR;
2031
2032 case MCK_VRNoV0:
2033 return B == MCK_VR;
2034
2035 case MCK_RVVMaskRegOpOperand:
2036 return B == OptionalMatchClass;
2037 }
2038}
2039
2040static unsigned validateOperandClass(MCParsedAsmOperand &GOp, MatchClassKind Kind) {
2041 RISCVOperand &Operand = (RISCVOperand &)GOp;
2042 if (Kind == InvalidMatchClass)
2043 return MCTargetAsmParser::Match_InvalidOperand;
2044
2045 if (Operand.isToken() && Kind <= MCK_LAST_TOKEN)
2046 return isSubclass(matchTokenString(Operand.getToken()), Kind) ?

2773 case RISCV::V22_V23_V24_V25_V26_V27_V28: OpKind = MCK_Reg54; break;
2774 case RISCV::V23_V24_V25_V26_V27_V28_V29: OpKind = MCK_Reg54; break;
2775 case RISCV::V24_V25_V26_V27_V28_V29_V30: OpKind = MCK_Reg54; break;
2776 case RISCV::V25_V26_V27_V28_V29_V30_V31: OpKind = MCK_Reg54; break;
2777 case RISCV::V0_V1_V2_V3_V4_V5_V6_V7: OpKind = MCK_Reg55; break;
2778 case RISCV::V1_V2_V3_V4_V5_V6_V7_V8: OpKind = MCK_Reg57; break;
2779 case RISCV::V2_V3_V4_V5_V6_V7_V8_V9: OpKind = MCK_Reg57; break;
2780 case RISCV::V3_V4_V5_V6_V7_V8_V9_V10: OpKind = MCK_Reg57; break;
2781 case RISCV::V4_V5_V6_V7_V8_V9_V10_V11: OpKind = MCK_Reg57; break;
2782 case RISCV::V5_V6_V7_V8_V9_V10_V11_V12: OpKind = MCK_Reg57; break;
2783 case RISCV::V6_V7_V8_V9_V10_V11_V12_V13: OpKind = MCK_Reg57; break;
2784 case RISCV::V7_V8_V9_V10_V11_V12_V13_V14: OpKind = MCK_Reg57; break;
2785 case RISCV::V8_V9_V10_V11_V12_V13_V14_V15: OpKind = MCK_Reg57; break;
2786 case RISCV::V9_V10_V11_V12_V13_V14_V15_V16: OpKind = MCK_Reg57; break;
2787 case RISCV::V10_V11_V12_V13_V14_V15_V16_V17: OpKind = MCK_Reg57; break;
2788 case RISCV::V11_V12_V13_V14_V15_V16_V17_V18: OpKind = MCK_Reg57; break;
2789 case RISCV::V12_V13_V14_V15_V16_V17_V18_V19: OpKind = MCK_Reg57; break;
2790 case RISCV::V13_V14_V15_V16_V17_V18_V19_V20: OpKind = MCK_Reg57; break;
2791 case RISCV::V14_V15_V16_V17_V18_V19_V20_V21: OpKind = MCK_Reg57; break;
2792 case RISCV::V15_V16_V17_V18_V19_V20_V21_V22: OpKind = MCK_Reg57; break;
2793 case RISCV::V16_V17_V18_V19_V20_V21_V22_V23: OpKind = MCK_Reg57; break;
2794 case RISCV::V17_V18_V19_V20_V21_V22_V23_V24: OpKind = MCK_Reg57; break;
2795 case RISCV::V18_V19_V20_V21_V22_V23_V24_V25: OpKind = MCK_Reg57; break;
2796 case RISCV::V19_V20_V21_V22_V23_V24_V25_V26: OpKind = MCK_Reg57; break;
2797 case RISCV::V20_V21_V22_V23_V24_V25_V26_V27: OpKind = MCK_Reg57; break;
2798 case RISCV::V21_V22_V23_V24_V25_V26_V27_V28: OpKind = MCK_Reg57; break;
2799 case RISCV::V22_V23_V24_V25_V26_V27_V28_V29: OpKind = MCK_Reg57; break;
2800 case RISCV::V23_V24_V25_V26_V27_V28_V29_V30: OpKind = MCK_Reg57; break;
2801 case RISCV::V24_V25_V26_V27_V28_V29_V30_V31: OpKind = MCK_Reg57; break;
2802 }
2803 return isSubclass(OpKind, Kind) ? (unsigned)MCTargetAsmParser::Match_Success :
2804 getDiagKindFromRegisterClass(Kind);
2805 }
2806
2807 if (Kind > MCK_LAST_TOKEN && Kind <= MCK_LAST_REGISTER)
2808 return getDiagKindFromRegisterClass(Kind);
2809
2810 return MCTargetAsmParser::Match_InvalidOperand;
2811}

2919FeatureBitset RISCVAsmParser::
2920ComputeAvailableFeatures(const FeatureBitset &FB) const {
2921 FeatureBitset Features;
2922 if (FB[RISCV::FeatureStdExtM])
2923 Features.set(Feature_HasStdExtMBit);
2924 if (FB[RISCV::FeatureStdExtA])
2925 Features.set(Feature_HasStdExtABit);
2926 if (FB[RISCV::FeatureStdExtF])
2927 Features.set(Feature_HasStdExtFBit);
2928 if (FB[RISCV::FeatureStdExtD])
2929 Features.set(Feature_HasStdExtDBit);
2930 if (FB[RISCV::FeatureExtZfh])
2931 Features.set(Feature_HasStdExtZfhBit);
2932 if (FB[RISCV::FeatureStdExtC])
2933 Features.set(Feature_HasStdExtCBit);
2934 if (FB[RISCV::FeatureExtZba])
2935 Features.set(Feature_HasStdExtZbaBit);
2936 if (FB[RISCV::FeatureExtZbb])
2937 Features.set(Feature_HasStdExtZbbBit);
2938 if (FB[RISCV::FeatureExtZbc])
2939 Features.set(Feature_HasStdExtZbcBit);
2940 if (FB[RISCV::FeatureExtZbe])
2941 Features.set(Feature_HasStdExtZbeBit);
2942 if (FB[RISCV::FeatureExtZbf])
2943 Features.set(Feature_HasStdExtZbfBit);
2944 if (FB[RISCV::FeatureExtZbm])
2945 Features.set(Feature_HasStdExtZbmBit);
2946 if (FB[RISCV::FeatureExtZbp])
2947 Features.set(Feature_HasStdExtZbpBit);
2948 if (FB[RISCV::FeatureExtZbr])
2949 Features.set(Feature_HasStdExtZbrBit);
2950 if (FB[RISCV::FeatureExtZbs])
2951 Features.set(Feature_HasStdExtZbsBit);
2952 if (FB[RISCV::FeatureExtZbt])
2953 Features.set(Feature_HasStdExtZbtBit);
2954 if ((FB[RISCV::FeatureExtZbb] || FB[RISCV::FeatureExtZbp]))
2955 Features.set(Feature_HasStdExtZbbOrZbpBit);
2956 if (FB[RISCV::FeatureExtZbproposedc])
2957 Features.set(Feature_HasStdExtZbproposedcBit);
2958 if (FB[RISCV::FeatureStdExtB])
2959 Features.set(Feature_HasStdExtBBit);
2960 if (!FB[RISCV::FeatureNoRVCHints])
2961 Features.set(Feature_HasRVCHintsBit);
2962 if (FB[RISCV::FeatureStdExtV])
2963 Features.set(Feature_HasStdExtVBit);
2964 if (FB[RISCV::FeatureStdExtZvlsseg])
2965 Features.set(Feature_HasStdExtZvlssegBit);
2966 if (FB[RISCV::FeatureExtZvamo])
2967 Features.set(Feature_HasStdExtZvamoBit);
2968 if (FB[RISCV::Feature64Bit])
2969 Features.set(Feature_IsRV64Bit);
2970 if (!FB[RISCV::Feature64Bit])
2971 Features.set(Feature_IsRV32Bit);
2972 if (FB[RISCV::FeatureRV32E])
2973 Features.set(Feature_IsRV32EBit);
2974 return Features;
2975}
2976
2977static bool checkAsmTiedOperandConstraints(const RISCVAsmParser&AsmParser,
2978 unsigned Kind,
2979 const OperandVector &Operands,
2980 uint64_t &ErrorInfo) {
2981 assert(Kind < CVT_NUM_SIGNATURES && "Invalid signature!");
2982 const uint8_t *Converter = ConversionTable[Kind];
2983 for (const uint8_t *p = Converter; *p; p += 2) {
2984 switch (*p) {
2985 case CVT_Tied: {
2986 unsigned OpIdx = *(p + 1);
2987 assert(OpIdx < (size_t)(std::end(TiedAsmOperandTable) -
2988 std::begin(TiedAsmOperandTable)) &&
2989 "Tied operand not found");
2990 unsigned OpndNum1 = TiedAsmOperandTable[OpIdx][1];
2991 unsigned OpndNum2 = TiedAsmOperandTable[OpIdx][2];
2992 if (OpndNum1 != OpndNum2) {
2993 auto &SrcOp1 = Operands[OpndNum1];
2994 auto &SrcOp2 = Operands[OpndNum2];
2995 if (SrcOp1->isReg() && SrcOp2->isReg()) {
2996 if (!AsmParser.regsEqual(*SrcOp1, *SrcOp2)) {
2997 ErrorInfo = OpndNum2;
2998 return false;
2999 }
3000 }
3001 }
3002 break;
3003 }
3004 default:
3005 break;
3006 }
3007 }
3008 return true;
3009}

3331namespace {
3332 struct MatchEntry {
3333 uint16_t Mnemonic;
3334 uint16_t Opcode;
3335 uint8_t ConvertFn;
3336 uint8_t RequiredFeaturesIdx;
3337 uint8_t Classes[7];
3338 StringRef getMnemonic() const {
3339 return StringRef(MnemonicTable + Mnemonic + 1,
3340 MnemonicTable[Mnemonic]);
3341 }
3342 };
3343
3344 // Predicate for searching for an opcode.
3345 struct LessOpcode {
3346 bool operator()(const MatchEntry &LHS, StringRef RHS) {
3347 return LHS.getMnemonic() < RHS;
3348 }
3349 bool operator()(StringRef LHS, const MatchEntry &RHS) {
3350 return LHS < RHS.getMnemonic();
3351 }
3352 bool operator()(const MatchEntry &LHS, const MatchEntry &RHS) {
3353 return LHS.getMnemonic() < RHS.getMnemonic();
3354 }
3355 };
3356} // end anonymous namespace

4815
4816#include "llvm/Support/Debug.h"
4817#include "llvm/Support/Format.h"
4818
4819unsigned RISCVAsmParser::
4820MatchInstructionImpl(const OperandVector &Operands,
4821 MCInst &Inst,
4822 uint64_t &ErrorInfo,
4823 FeatureBitset &MissingFeatures,
4824 bool matchingInlineAsm, unsigned VariantID) {
4825 // Eliminate obvious mismatches.
4826 if (Operands.size() > 8) {
4827 ErrorInfo = 8;
4828 return Match_InvalidOperand;
4829 }
4830
4831 // Get the current feature set.
4832 const FeatureBitset &AvailableFeatures = getAvailableFeatures();
4833
4834 // Get the instruction mnemonic, which is the first token.
4835 StringRef Mnemonic = ((RISCVOperand &)*Operands[0]).getToken();
4836
4837 // Process all MnemonicAliases to remap the mnemonic.
4838 applyMnemonicAliases(Mnemonic, AvailableFeatures, VariantID);
4839
4840 // Some state to try to produce better error messages.
4841 bool HadMatchOtherThanFeatures = false;
4842 bool HadMatchOtherThanPredicate = false;
4843 unsigned RetCode = Match_InvalidOperand;
4844 MissingFeatures.set();
4845 // Set ErrorInfo to the operand that mismatches if it is
4846 // wrong for all instances of the instruction.
4847 ErrorInfo = ~0ULL;
4848 SmallBitVector OptionalOperandsMask(7);
4849 // Find the appropriate table for this asm variant.
4850 const MatchEntry *Start, *End;
4851 switch (VariantID) {
4852 default: llvm_unreachable("invalid variant!");
4853 case 0: Start = std::begin(MatchTable0); End = std::end(MatchTable0); break;
4854 }
4855 // Search the table.
4856 auto MnemonicRange = std::equal_range(Start, End, Mnemonic, LessOpcode());
4857
4858 DEBUG_WITH_TYPE("asm-matcher", dbgs() << "AsmMatcher: found " <<
4859 std::distance(MnemonicRange.first, MnemonicRange.second) <<
4860 " encodings with mnemonic '" << Mnemonic << "'\n");
4861
4862 // Return a more specific error code if no mnemonics match.
4863 if (MnemonicRange.first == MnemonicRange.second)
4864 return Match_MnemonicFail;
4865
4866 for (const MatchEntry *it = MnemonicRange.first, *ie = MnemonicRange.second;
4867 it != ie; ++it) {
4868 const FeatureBitset &RequiredFeatures = FeatureBitsets[it->RequiredFeaturesIdx];
4869 bool HasRequiredFeatures =
4870 (AvailableFeatures & RequiredFeatures) == RequiredFeatures;
4871 DEBUG_WITH_TYPE("asm-matcher", dbgs() << "Trying to match opcode "
4872 << MII.getName(it->Opcode) << "\n");
4873 // equal_range guarantees that instruction mnemonic matches.
4874 assert(Mnemonic == it->getMnemonic());
4875 bool OperandsValid = true;
4876 OptionalOperandsMask.reset(0, 7);
4877 for (unsigned FormalIdx = 0, ActualIdx = 1; FormalIdx != 7; ++FormalIdx) {
4878 auto Formal = static_cast<MatchClassKind>(it->Classes[FormalIdx]);
4879 DEBUG_WITH_TYPE("asm-matcher",
4880 dbgs() << " Matching formal operand class " << getMatchClassName(Formal)
4881 << " against actual operand at index " << ActualIdx);
4882 if (ActualIdx < Operands.size())
4883 DEBUG_WITH_TYPE("asm-matcher", dbgs() << " (";
4884 Operands[ActualIdx]->print(dbgs()); dbgs() << "): ");
4885 else
4886 DEBUG_WITH_TYPE("asm-matcher", dbgs() << ": ");
4887 if (ActualIdx >= Operands.size()) {
4888 DEBUG_WITH_TYPE("asm-matcher", dbgs() << "actual operand index out of range ");
4889 OperandsValid = (Formal == InvalidMatchClass) || isSubclass(Formal, OptionalMatchClass);
4890 if (!OperandsValid) ErrorInfo = ActualIdx;
4891 OptionalOperandsMask.set(FormalIdx, 7);
4892 break;
4893 }
4894 MCParsedAsmOperand &Actual = *Operands[ActualIdx];
4895 unsigned Diag = validateOperandClass(Actual, Formal);
4896 if (Diag == Match_Success) {
4897 DEBUG_WITH_TYPE("asm-matcher",
4898 dbgs() << "match success using generic matcher\n");
4899 ++ActualIdx;
4900 continue;
4901 }
4902 // If the generic handler indicates an invalid operand
4903 // failure, check for a special case.
4904 if (Diag != Match_Success) {
4905 unsigned TargetDiag = validateTargetOperandClass(Actual, Formal);
4906 if (TargetDiag == Match_Success) {
4907 DEBUG_WITH_TYPE("asm-matcher",
4908 dbgs() << "match success using target matcher\n");
4909 ++ActualIdx;
4910 continue;
4911 }
4912 // If the target matcher returned a specific error code use
4913 // that, else use the one from the generic matcher.
4914 if (TargetDiag != Match_InvalidOperand && HasRequiredFeatures)
4915 Diag = TargetDiag;
4916 }
4917 // If current formal operand wasn't matched and it is optional
4918 // then try to match next formal operand
4919 if (Diag == Match_InvalidOperand && isSubclass(Formal, OptionalMatchClass)) {
4920 OptionalOperandsMask.set(FormalIdx);
4921 DEBUG_WITH_TYPE("asm-matcher", dbgs() << "ignoring optional operand\n");
4922 continue;
4923 }
4924 // If this operand is broken for all of the instances of this
4925 // mnemonic, keep track of it so we can report loc info.
4926 // If we already had a match that only failed due to a
4927 // target predicate, that diagnostic is preferred.
4928 if (!HadMatchOtherThanPredicate &&
4929 (it == MnemonicRange.first || ErrorInfo <= ActualIdx)) {
4930 if (HasRequiredFeatures && (ErrorInfo != ActualIdx || Diag != Match_InvalidOperand))
4931 RetCode = Diag;
4932 ErrorInfo = ActualIdx;
4933 }
4934 // Otherwise, just reject this instance of the mnemonic.
4935 OperandsValid = false;
4936 break;
4937 }
4938
4939 if (!OperandsValid) {
4940 DEBUG_WITH_TYPE("asm-matcher", dbgs() << "Opcode result: multiple "
4941 "operand mismatches, ignoring "
4942 "this opcode\n");
4943 continue;
4944 }
4945 if (!HasRequiredFeatures) {
4946 HadMatchOtherThanFeatures = true;
4947 FeatureBitset NewMissingFeatures = RequiredFeatures & ~AvailableFeatures;
4948 DEBUG_WITH_TYPE("asm-matcher", dbgs() << "Missing target features:";
4949 for (unsigned I = 0, E = NewMissingFeatures.size(); I != E; ++I)
4950 if (NewMissingFeatures[I])
4951 dbgs() << ' ' << I;
4952 dbgs() << "\n");
4953 if (NewMissingFeatures.count() <=
4954 MissingFeatures.count())
4955 MissingFeatures = NewMissingFeatures;
4956 continue;
4957 }
4958
4959 Inst.clear();
4960
4961 Inst.setOpcode(it->Opcode);
4962 // We have a potential match but have not rendered the operands.
4963 // Check the target predicate to handle any context sensitive
4964 // constraints.
4965 // For example, Ties that are referenced multiple times must be
4966 // checked here to ensure the input is the same for each match
4967 // constraints. If we leave it any later the ties will have been
4968 // canonicalized
4969 unsigned MatchResult;
4970 if ((MatchResult = checkEarlyTargetMatchPredicate(Inst, Operands)) != Match_Success) {
4971 Inst.clear();
4972 DEBUG_WITH_TYPE(
4973 "asm-matcher",
4974 dbgs() << "Early target match predicate failed with diag code "
4975 << MatchResult << "\n");
4976 RetCode = MatchResult;
4977 HadMatchOtherThanPredicate = true;
4978 continue;
4979 }
4980
4981 if (matchingInlineAsm) {
4982 convertToMapAndConstraints(it->ConvertFn, Operands);
4983 if (!checkAsmTiedOperandConstraints(*this, it->ConvertFn, Operands, ErrorInfo))
4984 return Match_InvalidTiedOperand;
4985
4986 return Match_Success;
4987 }
4988
4989 // We have selected a definite instruction, convert the parsed
4990 // operands into the appropriate MCInst.
4991 convertToMCInst(it->ConvertFn, Inst, it->Opcode, Operands,
4992 OptionalOperandsMask);
4993
4994 // We have a potential match. Check the target predicate to
4995 // handle any context sensitive constraints.
4996 if ((MatchResult = checkTargetMatchPredicate(Inst)) != Match_Success) {
4997 DEBUG_WITH_TYPE("asm-matcher",
4998 dbgs() << "Target match predicate failed with diag code "
4999 << MatchResult << "\n");
5000 Inst.clear();
5001 RetCode = MatchResult;
5002 HadMatchOtherThanPredicate = true;
5003 continue;
5004 }
5005
5006 if (!checkAsmTiedOperandConstraints(*this, it->ConvertFn, Operands, ErrorInfo))
5007 return Match_InvalidTiedOperand;
5008
5009 DEBUG_WITH_TYPE(
5010 "asm-matcher",
5011 dbgs() << "Opcode result: complete match, selecting this opcode\n");
5012 return Match_Success;
5013 }
5014
5015 // Okay, we had no match. Try to return a useful error code.
5016 if (HadMatchOtherThanPredicate || !HadMatchOtherThanFeatures)
5017 return RetCode;
5018
5019 ErrorInfo = 0;
5020 return Match_MissingFeature;
5021}
5022
5023namespace {
5024 struct OperandMatchEntry {
5025 uint16_t Mnemonic;
5026 uint8_t OperandMask;
5027 uint8_t Class;
5028 uint8_t RequiredFeaturesIdx;
5029
5030 StringRef getMnemonic() const {
5031 return StringRef(MnemonicTable + Mnemonic + 1,
5032 MnemonicTable[Mnemonic]);
5033 }
5034 };
5035
5036 // Predicate for searching for an opcode.
5037 struct LessOpcodeOperand {
5038 bool operator()(const OperandMatchEntry &LHS, StringRef RHS) {
5039 return LHS.getMnemonic() < RHS;
5040 }
5041 bool operator()(StringRef LHS, const OperandMatchEntry &RHS) {
5042 return LHS < RHS.getMnemonic();
5043 }
5044 bool operator()(const OperandMatchEntry &LHS, const OperandMatchEntry &RHS) {
5045 return LHS.getMnemonic() < RHS.getMnemonic();
5046 }
5047 };
5048} // end anonymous namespace
5049
5050static const OperandMatchEntry OperandMatchTable[792] = {
5051 /* Operand List Mnemonic, Mask, Operand Class, Features */
5052 { 0 /* add */, 8 /* 3 */, MCK_TPRelAddSymbol, AMFBS_None },
5053 { 27 /* amoadd.d */, 4 /* 2 */, MCK_AtomicMemOpOperand, AMFBS_HasStdExtA_IsRV64 },
5054 { 36 /* amoadd.d.aq */, 4 /* 2 */, MCK_AtomicMemOpOperand, AMFBS_HasStdExtA_IsRV64 },
5055 { 48 /* amoadd.d.aqrl */, 4 /* 2 */, MCK_AtomicMemOpOperand, AMFBS_HasStdExtA_IsRV64 },

5836 { 11628 /* vwsubu.wv */, 8 /* 3 */, MCK_RVVMaskRegOpOperand, AMFBS_HasStdExtV },
5837 { 11638 /* vwsubu.wx */, 8 /* 3 */, MCK_RVVMaskRegOpOperand, AMFBS_HasStdExtV },
5838 { 11648 /* vxor.vi */, 8 /* 3 */, MCK_RVVMaskRegOpOperand, AMFBS_HasStdExtV },
5839 { 11656 /* vxor.vv */, 8 /* 3 */, MCK_RVVMaskRegOpOperand, AMFBS_HasStdExtV },
5840 { 11664 /* vxor.vx */, 8 /* 3 */, MCK_RVVMaskRegOpOperand, AMFBS_HasStdExtV },
5841 { 11672 /* vzext.vf2 */, 4 /* 2 */, MCK_RVVMaskRegOpOperand, AMFBS_HasStdExtV },
5842 { 11682 /* vzext.vf4 */, 4 /* 2 */, MCK_RVVMaskRegOpOperand, AMFBS_HasStdExtV },
5843 { 11692 /* vzext.vf8 */, 4 /* 2 */, MCK_RVVMaskRegOpOperand, AMFBS_HasStdExtV },
5844};
5845
5846OperandMatchResultTy RISCVAsmParser::
5847tryCustomParseOperand(OperandVector &Operands,
5848 unsigned MCK) {
5849
5850 switch(MCK) {
5851 case MCK_AtomicMemOpOperand:
5852 return parseAtomicMemOp(Operands);
5853 case MCK_BareSymbol:
5854 return parseBareSymbol(Operands);
5855 case MCK_CSRSystemRegister:
5856 return parseCSRSystemRegister(Operands);
5857 case MCK_CallSymbol:
5858 return parseCallSymbol(Operands);
5859 case MCK_PseudoJumpSymbol:
5860 return parsePseudoJumpSymbol(Operands);
5861 case MCK_SImm21Lsb0JAL:
5862 return parseJALOffset(Operands);
5863 case MCK_TPRelAddSymbol:
5864 return parseOperandWithModifier(Operands);
5865 case MCK_RVVMaskRegOpOperand:
5866 return parseMaskReg(Operands);
5867 case MCK_VTypeI:
5868 return parseVTypeI(Operands);
5869 default:
5870 return MatchOperand_NoMatch;
5871 }
5872 return MatchOperand_NoMatch;
5873}
5874
5875OperandMatchResultTy RISCVAsmParser::
5876MatchOperandParserImpl(OperandVector &Operands,
5877 StringRef Mnemonic,
5878 bool ParseForAllFeatures) {
5879 // Get the current feature set.
5880 const FeatureBitset &AvailableFeatures = getAvailableFeatures();
5881
5882 // Get the next operand index.
5883 unsigned NextOpNum = Operands.size() - 1;
5884 // Search the table.
5885 auto MnemonicRange =
5886 std::equal_range(std::begin(OperandMatchTable), std::end(OperandMatchTable),
5887 Mnemonic, LessOpcodeOperand());
5888
5889 if (MnemonicRange.first == MnemonicRange.second)
5890 return MatchOperand_NoMatch;
5891
5892 for (const OperandMatchEntry *it = MnemonicRange.first,
5893 *ie = MnemonicRange.second; it != ie; ++it) {
5894 // equal_range guarantees that instruction mnemonic matches.
5895 assert(Mnemonic == it->getMnemonic());
5896
5897 // check if the available features match
5898 const FeatureBitset &RequiredFeatures = FeatureBitsets[it->RequiredFeaturesIdx];
5899 if (!ParseForAllFeatures && (AvailableFeatures & RequiredFeatures) != RequiredFeatures)
5900 continue;
5901
5902 // check if the operand in question has a custom parser.
5903 if (!(it->OperandMask & (1 << NextOpNum)))
5904 continue;
5905
5906 // call custom parse method to handle the operand
5907 OperandMatchResultTy Result = tryCustomParseOperand(Operands, it->Class);
5908 if (Result != MatchOperand_NoMatch)
5909 return Result;
5910 }
5911
5912 // Okay, we had no match.
5913 return MatchOperand_NoMatch;
5914}
5915
5916#endif // GET_MATCHER_IMPLEMENTATION
5917
5918
5919#ifdef GET_MNEMONIC_SPELL_CHECKER
5920#undef GET_MNEMONIC_SPELL_CHECKER
5921
5922static std::string RISCVMnemonicSpellCheck(StringRef S, const FeatureBitset &FBS, unsigned VariantID) {
5923 const unsigned MaxEditDist = 2;
5924 std::vector<StringRef> Candidates;
5925 StringRef Prev = "";
5926
5927 // Find the appropriate table for this asm variant.
5928 const MatchEntry *Start, *End;
5929 switch (VariantID) {
5930 default: llvm_unreachable("invalid variant!");
5931 case 0: Start = std::begin(MatchTable0); End = std::end(MatchTable0); break;
5932 }
5933
5934 for (auto I = Start; I < End; I++) {
5935 // Ignore unsupported instructions.
5936 const FeatureBitset &RequiredFeatures = FeatureBitsets[I->RequiredFeaturesIdx];
5937 if ((FBS & RequiredFeatures) != RequiredFeatures)
5938 continue;
5939
5940 StringRef T = I->getMnemonic();
5941 // Avoid recomputing the edit distance for the same string.
5942 if (T.equals(Prev))
5943 continue;
5944
5945 Prev = T;
5946 unsigned Dist = S.edit_distance(T, false, MaxEditDist);
5947 if (Dist <= MaxEditDist)
5948 Candidates.push_back(T);
5949 }
5950
5951 if (Candidates.empty())
5952 return "";
5953
5954 std::string Res = ", did you mean: ";
5955 unsigned i = 0;
5956 for (; i < Candidates.size() - 1; i++)
5957 Res += Candidates[i].str() + ", ";
5958 return Res + Candidates[i].str() + "?";
5959}
5960
5961#endif // GET_MNEMONIC_SPELL_CHECKER
5962
5963
5964#ifdef GET_MNEMONIC_CHECKER
5965#undef GET_MNEMONIC_CHECKER
5966
5967static bool RISCVCheckMnemonic(StringRef Mnemonic,
5968 const FeatureBitset &AvailableFeatures,
5969 unsigned VariantID) {
5970 // Process all MnemonicAliases to remap the mnemonic.
5971 applyMnemonicAliases(Mnemonic, AvailableFeatures, VariantID);
5972
5973 // Find the appropriate table for this asm variant.
5974 const MatchEntry *Start, *End;
5975 switch (VariantID) {
5976 default: llvm_unreachable("invalid variant!");
5977 case 0: Start = std::begin(MatchTable0); End = std::end(MatchTable0); break;
5978 }
5979
5980 // Search the table.
5981 auto MnemonicRange = std::equal_range(Start, End, Mnemonic, LessOpcode());
5982
5983 if (MnemonicRange.first == MnemonicRange.second)
5984 return false;
5985
5986 for (const MatchEntry *it = MnemonicRange.first, *ie = MnemonicRange.second;
5987 it != ie; ++it) {
5988 const FeatureBitset &RequiredFeatures =
5989 FeatureBitsets[it->RequiredFeaturesIdx];
5990 if ((AvailableFeatures & RequiredFeatures) == RequiredFeatures)
5991 return true;
5992 }
5993 return false;
5994}
5995
5996#endif // GET_MNEMONIC_CHECKER
